The Gazette of the Democratic Socialist Republic of Sri Lanka
(Published by Authority)
PART IV (B) — LOCAL  GOVERNMENT
Local  Government  Notiﬁ cations
1A- PG 6276 - 07 (03/2023) 
This Gazette Extraordinary can be downloaded from www.documents.gov.lk
PRADESHIYA SABHA BINGIRIYA
THE notiﬁ cation and road schedule published under the Section IV (B), local government notiﬁ cations in the Extraordinary 
Gazette of the Democratic Socialist Republic of Sri Lanka  dated Thursday, 07th April 2022 bearing number 2274/20 is 
hereby cancelled. Instead it is announced to the public that the following notiﬁ cation and resolution will be published here.
IT is hereby notiﬁed for the public information that it has been decided under the resolution No. 04/2023/02/05-VIII moved 
at the General Conference held on 14.02.2023 at the Pradeshiya Sabha, Bingiriya that the Roads and Lanes included in 
the following Schedule should be declared as roads and Lanes owned by the Bingiriya Pradeshiya Sabha, in terms of the 
functions assigned to the Pradeshiya Sabhas in the North Western Province by the series of "Orders regarding the preparation 
of plans for the roads and lanes maintained by the Pradeshiya Sabha in the North Western Province and the publication of 
advertisements showing the names of roads and lanes" published by the Hon. Governor, North Western Province in the 
Extraordinary Gazette No. 2238/35 dated 30th,  July 2021 to be read with Section 24 of the Pradeshiya Sabha Act, No. 15 
of 1987. 
 If it is the opinion of the claimant party that any road or lane included in the said schedule will pass through any land or 
include in any part of a land, action should be taken to ﬁle a case in a proper court within three months from the date of this 
notiﬁcation is published in order to conﬁrm his ownership of that land.
 It is further noti ﬁed that all the roads and lanes included in the schedule for which cases have not been ﬁled in the Court 
before the expiry of the said period of three months will be considered as roads and lanes owned by the Bingiriya Pradeshiya 
Sabha.
K. R. P. G. R. K
ARUNANAYAKE,
Secretary, 
Bingiriya Pradeshiya Sabha.
At Bingiriya Pradeshiya Sabha Head Ofﬁ ce,
23rd of March 2023.

2AResolution
Bingiriya Pradeshiya Sabha proposes that the Roads and lanes mentioned in the list included in the following schedule should be considered as Roads and lanes 
maintained by the Bingiriya Pradeshiya Sabha under the provisions of the series of "Orders regarding the preparation of plans for the Roads and lanes maintained 
by the Pradeshiya Sabhas in the North Western Province and the publication of advertisements showing the names of Roads and lanes" published by the Hon. 
Governor, North Western Province in the Extraordinary Gazette Notiﬁcation No. 2238/35 dated 30th July, 2021, and the provisions of Section 24 (1) of the 
Pradeshiya Sabha Act, No. 15 of 1987.
